CRITIC.RESPONSE
The rating is 8 of 10. 
The play-by-play data looks generally good and well-formatted.  It accurately captures when each player enters and leaves the game. The only issue is there is some minor formatting and data quality issues.  
1) The 'wctimestring' column seems to be repeating time, and there is no need for this extra time information as it does not change between rows.  This extra column could have been omitted
2) The 'player1_team_abbreviation' and 'player2_team_abbreviation' columns are sometimes missing or are not clear on which player it is referring to.  This was a very small issue.  It may be a good idea to make sure these columns are always present. 
3) The 'neutraldescription' column could be improved upon.  For example the row where a player misses a shot would be good to have an extra column for this data.  
4) The 'REBOUND' rows would be good to have an extra column for if the rebound was an offensive rebound or defensive rebound
5)  It is difficult to tell if the players are starting or stopping playing.  It would have been a good idea to include 'starts' and 'stops' in the 'neutraldescription' column
